 dilli-ensiaar ke zyaadaatar ilaakon main 3 oktober se aasmaan par badalon kii awajahi ke bich halki barish kii sambhaavna bad jaaegi
 The Meteorological Department says that the weather will remain pleasant in all areas of the capital from October 3 to 5
 aasmaan parabadalonki awajahi ke bich halki phuhaaron ke saath dhoop-chhaanv kaa silsilaa dekha jayega
 Due to this, there will be a possibility of a drop in day temperature
 western disterbence kaa dikhegaa asaradrasal uttar pashchim bharat ke zyaadaatar ilaakon main pichley 10 dinon se aasmaan saaf he or pashchim disha se chal rahi hawaaon ne jor pakad liya he
 Due to the sunshine, day temperatures are above normal in most areas
 mausam vibhaag ke diarector aar vishen ke mutabik aktubar main teen taarikh se uttar bharat main ek western disterbence kaa asar dikhne ja rahaa he or isi samay yahaan par easterli wave apane saath nam hawaaen lekar bhi pahunch rahi he
 Therefore, the Meteorological Department is expressing the possibility of reconciliation between the two weather systems
 western disterbence or easterli wave ke chalate rajdhani dilli ke saath-saath haryana, himachal, pashchimi uttar pradesh or uttarakhand ke aasmaan par badalon kaa deraa ho jayega
 Due to this, Uttarakhand will see moderate rainfall
 himachal pradesh ke us ilaake main barish hogi, jo uttarakhand se lagata he
 The weather department is expecting light rain in Haryana, Delhi and western Uttar Pradesh
 sabase zyada asar uttarakhand menmausam vibhaag ke mutabik western disterbence ke chalate jammu-kashmir kii oonchi pahadiyon par mausam jarur badalegaa lekin iskaa mukhya asar uttarakhand main hi dekha jayega
 The special thing is that the monsoon winds have started to bid farewell to all areas of northwest India
 aise main aane vaale dinon main western disterbence kaa jor uttar bharat main bad jayega
 According to experts, this time there is a lot of possibility of western disturbance activity, but it is not possible to say how cold it will be due to this
 amritsar haadase ko lekar aarope-pratyarope ke bich dashahra kaarykram ke aayojakon or mukhya atithinvajot corsiddhu ke khilaaf bihar kii ek adaalat main somvaar ko ek maamla daayar kiya gaya he
 At the same time, the National Human Rights Commission (NHRC) issued notice to the Railways and the Punjab Government
 dashahra ke din amritsar main ravan dahan ke dauraan train kii chapet main aane se 59 logon kii maut ho gai thi
 Among the dead were migrants from Bihar
 siddhu ke bachaav main congress saansad sunil jakhad or punjab ke mantri trupt rajinder singh bajva aage aae or unhone ghatana ke liye rail adhikariyon ko doshi tehraane kii koshish kii

 siem ne kii samiksha baithkais bich punjab ke mukhyamantri amarinder singh isroyal gaye hue hai

 The angry people pelted stones on Sunday and also had a clash with the workers
 ve patariyon par baith gaye the jahaan haadasa hua, baad main unhen adhikariyon kii ore se hataaya gaya, tab jaakar root par rail seva behaal ho pai
 Negligence of administration: National Human Rights Commission on Monday issued notice to Railway and Punjab Government regarding Amritsar accident
 notice jari karte hue ayog ne kaha ki rail patariyon par logon ke baithne ko samajhadaari bharaa kaam nahin kaha ja saktaa lekin saath hi is bhayaavah ghatana ke peeche jile ke adhikariyon kii laaparvaahee saaf dikhti he

 enechaarsi ne media main ai khabaron kaa sangyaan liya

 mukhya nyaayik magistrate kii adaalat main ek saamaajik kaaryakarta tamanna hashmi kii ore se pariwaad patr daayar kiya gaya

 unhone pariwaad patr main aarope lagaaya cor kii maujuudagi ke kaaran kaarykram main kaaphi log jamaa hue the

 hashmi ne cor par gaiyr jimmedaarana krity karne or kartavyon kaa nirvahan nahin karne kaa aarope lagaate hue unke khilaaf karrwai kiye jane kii maang kii he
 Navjot Sidhu, a minister in the Siddhupanjab government with the victims, has announced in a press conference on Monday that he will bear the responsibility of the orphaned children in the accident

 tippaniyan By the way, Sanjay's life has been full of ups and downs, so let's take a look at his life on his birthday
 
 
 29 july, 1959 ko janme sanjay dutt abhinayta sunil dutt or abhinetri naragis dutt ke teen bacchon main sabase bade hai
 Sanjay did his schooling at The Lawrence School in Sanawar, near Kasauli
 sanjay dutt kii priya or namrata naam kii do bahanen hai
 Priya is a politician and is married to Owen Roncon, while Namrata is married to actor Kumar Gaurav
 sanjay dutt 12 saal kii umr main pehali baar filmon main najar aae the
 In the 1971 Sunil Dutt film Reshma Aur Shera, Sanjay Qawwali was seen in a small role as a singer
 film main wahidaa rahamaan or raakhi ne bhi kaam kiya tha
 At the age of 22, father Sunil Dutt launched Sanjay in 'rocky', which was very liked
 haalanki film kii release se mahaz teen din pehle cancer se peedit sanjay kii maa naragis kaa nidhan ho gaya tha
 After doing a number of hits and flops, Sanjay Dutt acted in 1986's Naam, which was his first critically successful film
 is film main unke bahanoi kumaar gaurav ne bhi kaam kiya tha
 The '90s can be called the era of Sanjay Dutt's success
 is dauraan unhone 'khalanaayak' or 'sadak' ke alaava 'thanedaar' (1990), 'khun kaa karj' (1991), 'yalgaar' (1992), 'gumraah' (1993), 'sahiban' (1993) or 'aatish' jaisi filmein kin
 In the year 1991 Saajan, Sanjay played the role of a poet, changing his image of action hero
 film main unke saath maadhuri dikshit or salmaan khan pramukh bhoomikaaon main the
 He received his first Filmfare Award in the 'best Actor' category for this role
 varsh 1993 main sanjay dutt ko avaidh tareeke se hathiyaar rakhane ke aarope main giraftaar kiya gaya
 After this he remained in jail for about 18 months
 giraftaar ke teen saptaah baad 'khalanaayak' release hui, is film main maadhuri dikshit or jaiki shroff unke sahakalakaar the
 The film was a super hit and Sanjay was counted among the top Bollywood actors
 jail se baahar aane ke baad sanjay dutt ne 1999 main 'khubasurat', 'daag : da fire', 'hasina maan jaaegi' or award vining 'vastav' se filmon main vaapasi kii
 Sanjay Dutt played a gangster in 'vaastav', for which he was again given the Filmfare Award as Best Actor
 jis film ne sanjay dutt ko nai pahchaan di, vah 2003 main ai 'munnabhai MBBS' or 2006 main ai uski sikwel 'lage raho munnabhai' thim

 is film ke baad sanjay dutt kii comic timming ko kaaphi saraahna mili

 amitabh bachchan kii 1990 kii superhit film 'agnipath' ke 2012 main aae isi naam ke rimek ne pehle din kii kamai ke saare record tod die

 Patanjali was founded in the year 2006 in collaboration with yoga guru Baba Ramdev, who manufactures everything from shampoo to dental hygiene (also toothpaste)
 
 
 pichley saal 5,000 karod rupee ke kaarobaar kaa aankada paar kar lene vaale ayurveda ke is samrajya main baba ramdev kii bhale hi koi hissedari nahin he, lekin iskaa cheharaa vahi hai
 
 
 Baba Ramdev, face of Patanjali, has no stake in this business of Balakrishna agar shaan-o-shaukat kii baat karen, to daftar main maujuud baalkrishna ke aasapaas sirf kaale-safed rang kii ek rangerovar car nazar aati he, jisase vah ghar se daftar aate-jate hai, yaa patanjali parisar ke ek hisse se duusare main jaaya karte hai, kyonki haridwar main bana yah parisar 150 acre main failaa hua he
 
 
 Asked if he enjoys a comfortable ride, his answer was, "don't think about the car, it's better to think about safety
" 
 
 " is par baba ramdev ne kaha, "maine unhen majaboor kiya tha ki yahi car khariden

 ham mahangi chizon kii parvaah nahin karte
 
 
 "with this, he also showed a very simple mobile phone, which according to him was Rs 2,000
 
 
 haalanki baalkrishna ne sweekaar kiya ki unke paas yphone he
 
 
 The two friends first met 30 years ago in Gurukul, Haryana, where they studied, and soon became close to each other
 
 
 baalkrishna sharmile hai, baba ramdev media-friendli hai
 
 
 Balkrishna is somewhat obese, while Baba Ramdev can easily perform even the toughest asanas with the help of his thin body in front of hundreds of thousands of people or TV cameras
 
 
 unka kaamkaaji rishta bhi bilkul anoothaa he
 
 
 Baba Ramdev calls his closest colleague a 'spiritual partner, not a business partner', while Balakrishna says, "there is nothing like a board meeting between us
" 
 
 kabhi-kabhi vah mere paas koi idia lekar aate hai, or vah pehle se jaanate hai ki mujhe kya chahie

 tippaniyan On Wednesday night, Chavan held a high-level meeting with the chief secretary and top police officials, official sources said

 is bich, shivasena ke pravaktaa sanjay raut ne kaha ki bal thakare philhal jivan rakshak pranali par nahin hai

 unhone samvaadadaataaon se kaha, kal raat jivan rakshak pranali kii jarurat padi thi, lekin aaj uski jarurat nahin rahi
 Meanwhile, no bulletin has been released regarding the health of Bal Thackeray
